Proof:

After renaming modulo the bijection { a ↦ 0, b ↦ 1, c ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 ⟶ ,
  0 1 ⟶ ,
  0 2 2 ⟶ 2 2 1 0 2 0 }

Reversing the system.
After renaming modulo the bijection { 0 ↦ 0, 1 ↦ 1, 2 ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 ⟶ ,
  1 0 ⟶ ,
  2 2 0 ⟶ 0 2 0 1 2 2 }

Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
  Here, ↑ marks so-called defined symbols.
After renaming modulo the bijection { (2,↑) ↦ 0, (2,↓) ↦ 1, (0,↓) ↦ 2, (0,↑) ↦ 3, (1,↓) ↦ 4, (1,↑) ↦ 5 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 9-rules system (6 strict rules)
{ 0 1 2 ⟶ 3 1 2 4 1 1 ,
  0 1 2 ⟶ 0 2 4 1 1 ,
  0 1 2 ⟶ 3 4 1 1 ,
  0 1 2 ⟶ 5 1 1 ,
  0 1 2 ⟶ 0 1 ,
  0 1 2 ⟶ 0 ,
  2 →= ,
  4 2 →= ,
  1 1 2 →= 2 1 2 4 1 1 }

Removing 3 rules by a matrix interpretation [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006]
  of type E_J with J = {1,...,2} and dimension 2:

    ⎜ 1 1 ⎟
    ⎜ 0 1 ⎟
    ⎝     ⎠

    ⎜ 0 1 ⎟
    ⎝     ⎠

5 ↦ ⎛     ⎞
    ⎜ 1 0 ⎟
    ⎜ 0 1 ⎟
    ⎝     ⎠
